üí¨ Supervisor Agent Output:
  I\'ll help you optimize the machine assignments and resolve the identified bottlenecks. Let me apply advanced bottleneck scheduling techniques to improve the current schedule.\n\n## Bottleneck Analysis & Optimization Strategy\n\n### 1. Current Bottleneck Assessment\n\n**Primary Bottleneck: M28**\n- Utilization: 184 time units (31% of makespan)\n- Operations: 4 critical operations\n- Bottleneck Intensity: High (184/594 = 31%)\n\n**Secondary Bottlenecks:**\n- M61, M86, M98 (need specific utilization data)\n\n### 2. Theory of Constraints (TOC) Application\n\n```python\nclass BottleneckOptimizer:\n    def __init__(self, makespan=594, bottleneck_machine="M28", bottleneck_load=184):\n        self.current_makespan = makespan\n        self.bottleneck_machine = bottleneck_machine\n        self.bottleneck_load = bottleneck_load\n        self.target_improvement = 0.15  # 15% improvement target\n        \n    def calculate_bottleneck_metrics(self):\n        return {\n            \'bottleneck_utilization\': self.bottleneck_load / self.current_makespan,\n            \'theoretical_minimum\': max(self.bottleneck_load, self.current_makespan * 0.85),\n            \'improvement_potential\': self.current_makespan - self.bottleneck_load\n        }\n```\n\n### 3.
